                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">صدّقهُ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form>, (S, M, O, &amp;c.,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">تَصْدِيقٌ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">contr. of</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">كَذَّبَهُ</foreign>. (O, * K.) [This explanation implies several meanings here following.] <hi rend="ital">He attributed,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">ascribed, to him truth, veracity,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the speaking truth.</hi> (Msb.) And <hi rend="ital">He said to him,</hi> “ <hi rend="ital">Thou hast spoken truth.</hi> ” (Msb.) <hi rend="ital">He accepted,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">admitted,</hi> [or <hi rend="ital">assented to,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">believed,</hi>] <hi rend="ital">what he said:</hi> (M:) you say, <foreign lang="ar">صدّقهُ فِى حَدِيثِهِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He accepted,</hi> &amp;c., <hi rend="ital">what he said in his information,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">narration</hi>]: (S:) and you say <foreign lang="ar">صدّق بِلِسَانِهِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He assented to the truth of what was said with his tongue</hi>]; as well as <foreign lang="ar">بِقَلْبِهِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">with his heart,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">mind</hi>]. (T in art. <foreign lang="ar">اَمن</foreign>.) <hi rend="ital">He held him to be a speaker of truth.</hi> (MA.) [<hi rend="ital">He found him to be a speaker of truth. He,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it, proved him to be a speaker of truth; verified him;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">confirmed the truth of what he said:</hi> see an ex. in a verse cited voce <foreign lang="ar">بَيْنٌ</foreign>.] <hi rend="ital">He found it</hi> (an opinion) <hi rend="ital">to be true,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">veritable.</hi> (Ksh and Bd and Jel, in xxxiv. 19.) <hi rend="ital">He verified it; confirmed its truth;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proved it to be true,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">veritable;</hi> i. e. an opinion [&amp;c.]; syn. <foreign lang="ar">حَقَّقَهُ</foreign>: (Ksh and Bd, ibid.:) one says, <foreign lang="ar">صَدَّقَ الخَبَرَ الخُبْرُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">The trial, proof,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">test, verified the information</hi>]. (S in art. <foreign lang="ar">خبر</foreign>.) See 1, near the end. In the saying in the Kur [xxxix. 34], <foreign lang="ar">وَٱلَّذِى جَآءَ بِالصِّدْقِ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">وَصَدَّقَ بِهِ</foreign>, [which seems to be best rendered <hi rend="ital">But he who hath brought the truth and</hi> he who <hi rend="ital">hath accepted it as the truth,</hi> (see <foreign lang="ar">كَذَّبَ بِالأَمْرِ</foreign>,)] 'Alee the son of Aboo-Tálib is related to have said that by <foreign lang="ar">الذى جآء بالصدق</foreign> is meant Mohammad; and by <foreign lang="ar">الذى صدّق به</foreign>, Aboo-Bekr: or, as some say, Gabriel and Mohammad [are meant by the former and the latter respectively]: or by the former, Mohammad; and by the latter, [every one of] the believers: (M:) accord. to Er-Rághib, by <foreign lang="ar">وصدّق به</foreign> is meant <hi rend="ital">and hath found,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proved, to be true</hi> (<foreign lang="ar">حَقَّقَ</foreign>) <hi rend="ital">that which he hath brought by word,</hi> by that which he hath aimed at (<foreign lang="ar">بِمَا تَحَرَّاهُ</foreign>) by deed. (TA.)          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">صدّق</foreign> is also said to signify <hi rend="ital">He said,</hi> “ This thing is the truth; ” like <foreign lang="ar">حَقَّقَ</foreign>. (TA in art. <foreign lang="ar">حق</foreign>.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  And this verb also denotes <foreign lang="ar">المُبَالَغَةُ فِى الصِّدْقِ</foreign>: thus in the saying, <quote>
                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">صَدَّقَتْ فِيهِمْ ظُنُونِى</foreign>
                     </L> 
                  </quote> [<hi rend="ital">My opinions respecting them were,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">proved to be, very true</hi> or <hi rend="ital">correct</hi>]. (Ksh, in xxxiv. 19.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">صدّق الوَحْشِىُّ</foreign>, (O, K, TA,) or   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n23997-1" target="صَدَقَ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n23996"/></foreign>, (so in a copy of the M,) <tropical>(tropical:)</tropical>  <hi rend="ital">The wild animal ran without looking aside, when charged upon,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">attacked:</hi> (M, O, K, TA:) mentioned by IDrd.                   <hi rend="ital">He exacted from them the poor-rate.</hi> (TA. [See <foreign lang="ar">صَدَقَةٌ</foreign>.])          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  See also 5.    </entryFree>26:T2213,<entryFree id="n23996" key="صَدَقَ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <itype>1</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">صَدَقَ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">ذ</orth>
                  </form>, (S, M, O, Msb, K,) aor.      
    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Bu" lang="ar">صَدُقَ</orth>
                  </form>, (M, TA,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">صِدْقٌ</foreign> (S, * M, O, * Msb, K, TA) and <foreign lang="ar">صَدْقٌ</foreign>, (M, K,) the former of which is the more chaste, (TA,) or the latter is an inf. n. and the former is a simple subst., (K,) and <foreign lang="ar">تَصْدَاقٌ</foreign> (M) and <foreign lang="ar">مَصْدُوقَةٌ</foreign>, (O, K, TA,) which is one of the [few] inf. ns. of the measure <foreign lang="ar">مَفْعُولَةٌ</foreign>, (O, TA,) [or a fem. pass. part. n. used as an inf. n. like as is said of its contr. <foreign lang="ar">مَكْذُوبَةٌ</foreign>,] <hi rend="ital">he spoke, said, uttered,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">told, truth,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">truly,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">veraciously; contr. of</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">كَذَبَ</foreign>: (Msb: [and in like manner it is said in the S and M and O and K that <foreign lang="ar">صِدْقٌ</foreign> is the <hi rend="ital">contr. of</hi> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">كَذِبٌ</foreign>:]) Er-Rághib says that <foreign lang="ar">صِدْقٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">كَذِبٌ</foreign> are primarily in what is said, whether relating to the past or to the future, and [in the latter case] whether it be a promise or other than a promise; and only in what is said in the way of information: but sometimes they are in other modes of speech, such as asking a question, and commanding, and supplicating; as when one says, “ Is Zeyd in the house? ” for this implies information of his being ignorant of the state of Zeyd; and when one says, “ Make me to share with thee, or to be equal with thee, ” for this implies his requiring to be made to share with the other, or to be made equal with him; and when one says, “ Do not thou hurt me, ” for this implies that the other is hurting him: <foreign lang="ar">صِدْقٌ</foreign>, he says, is [by implication] the agreeing of what is said with what is conceived in the mind and with the thing told of, together; otherwise it is not complete <foreign lang="ar">صِدْق</foreign>, but may be described either as <foreign lang="ar">صِدْق</foreign> or sometimes as <foreign lang="ar">صِدْق</foreign> and sometimes as <foreign lang="ar">كَذِب</foreign> according to two different points of view; as when one says without believing it, “ Mohammad is the Apostle of God, ” for this may be termed <foreign lang="ar">صِدْق</foreign> because what is told is such, and it may be termed <foreign lang="ar">كَذِب</foreign> because it is at variance with what the speaker conceives in his mind. (TA.) One says, <foreign lang="ar">صَدَقَ فِى الحَدِيثِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He spoke truth in the information,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">narration</hi>]. (S, O, K.) And <foreign lang="ar">صَدَقَهُ</foreign> i. e. <hi rend="ital">He told him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">informed him, with truth,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">veracity,</hi> (AHeyth, * M, Msb, *) <foreign lang="ar">فِى القَوْلِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">in the saying</hi>]; for it is trans. as well as intrans. (Msb.) And <foreign lang="ar">صَدَقَهُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الحَدِيثَ</foreign> (S, O, K, in the CK [erroneously] <foreign lang="ar">صَدَّقَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">فُلانًا الحَدِيثَ</foreign>) <hi rend="ital">He told him with truth,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">veracity, the information,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">narration;</hi> for it is sometimes doubly trans. (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">صَدَقَنِى سِنَّ بَكْرِهِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He hath told me truly the age,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">as to the age, of his youthful camel;</hi> or <foreign lang="ar">صَدَقَنِى سِنُّ بَكْرِهِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">the age of his youthful camel has spoken truly to me</hi>]: (S, O, K:) a prov., (S, O,) expl. in art. <foreign lang="ar">بكر</foreign> [q. v.]. (K.)
